class="[--thread-content-max-width:40rem] thread-lg:[--thread-content-max-width:48rem] mx-auto max-w-(--thread-content-max-width) flex-1 group/turn-messages focus-visible:outline-hidden relative flex class="whitespace-pre-wrap">I'm writing parser that is a statefull class, that processes incoming bytes and converts into ESC/POS command (which I call document elements)
intreface IEscPosParser
{
  void Feed(byte[] data)
  void Complete()
  List&lt;Element&gt; Document;
}

Element is a base class for all other element, that represent esc/pos data:
TextElement, BarcodeElement, QrcodeElement, PagecutElement, PulseElement, BellElement, RasterImageElement, etc. Each class contains corresponding properties, that match esc/pos protocol

Document data as byte array may come in parser not in one piece, but cut be chunked in any way with any timeouts between chunks.

My goal is to write effective IEscPosParser implementation.
Instead of explicitely iterating all possible ESC/POS in code, I want to split data and code. For that, I want to declare supported commands in List&lt;..&gt;

My first question to you: Ask what is missing in this description. Then rephrase this task with better english end technical terms.

From then, we will move further.

<h3 data-start="81" data-end="115"> Whats Missing or Ambiguous</h3>
<p data-start="117" data-end="228">To fully understand and design this parser, here are some details that would need to be specified or clarified:</p>
<ol data-start="230" data-end="1344">
<li data-start="230" data-end="433">
<p data-start="233" data-end="261"><strong data-start="233" data-end="261">Command definition model</strong></p>
<ul data-start="265" data-end="433">
<li data-start="265" data-end="337">
<p data-start="267" data-end="337">How exactly are ESC/POS commands represented in your declarative list?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="341" data-end="433">
<p data-start="343" data-end="433">Is there a structure (e.g., command prefix, parameters, handler) defined for each command?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="435" data-end="636">
<p data-start="438" data-end="458"><strong data-start="438" data-end="458">State management</strong></p>
<ul data-start="462" data-end="636">
<li data-start="462" data-end="569">
<p data-start="464" data-end="569">What states does the parser maintain (e.g., idle, reading command, reading parameters, waiting for data)?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="573" data-end="636">
<p data-start="575" data-end="636">How are incomplete sequences buffered between <code data-start="621" data-end="629">Feed()</code> calls?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="638" data-end="809">
<p data-start="641" data-end="659"><strong data-start="641" data-end="659">Error handling</strong></p>
<ul data-start="663" data-end="809">
<li data-start="663" data-end="733">
<p data-start="665" data-end="733">What happens if the parser receives an unknown or malformed command?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="737" data-end="809">
<p data-start="739" data-end="809">Should it skip invalid bytes, raise an error, or try to resynchronize?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="811" data-end="926">
<p data-start="814" data-end="846"><strong data-start="814" data-end="846">Thread-safety and reentrancy</strong></p>
<ul data-start="850" data-end="926">
<li data-start="850" data-end="926">
<p data-start="852" data-end="926">Is the parser expected to be used from multiple threads or asynchronously?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="928" data-end="1090">
<p data-start="931" data-end="960"><strong data-start="931" data-end="960">Encoding and localization</strong></p>
<ul data-start="964" data-end="1090">
<li data-start="964" data-end="1021">
<p data-start="966" data-end="1021">How are text encodings handled (ESC/POS supports many)?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1025" data-end="1090">
<p data-start="1027" data-end="1090">Should the parser decode characters or just preserve raw bytes?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="1092" data-end="1225">
<p data-start="1095" data-end="1111"><strong data-start="1095" data-end="1111">Output model</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1115" data-end="1225">
<li data-start="1115" data-end="1225">
<p data-start="1117" data-end="1225">Are elements added to the <code data-start="1143" data-end="1153">Document</code> immediately as commands complete, or only after <code data-start="1202" data-end="1214">Complete()</code> is called?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="1227" data-end="1344">
<p data-start="1230" data-end="1250"><strong data-start="1230" data-end="1250">Command coverage</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1254" data-end="1344">
<li data-start="1254" data-end="1344">
<p data-start="1256" data-end="1344">Which ESC/POS command families must be supported (text, image, barcodes, control, etc.)?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="1346" data-end="1349">
<h3 data-start="1351" data-end="1408"> Rephrased Task (Clearer English &amp; Technical Terms)</h3>
<blockquote data-start="1410" data-end="2949">
<p data-start="1412" data-end="1555"><strong data-start="1412" data-end="1421">Goal:</strong><br data-start="1421" data-end="1424">
Implement a robust, stateful ESC/POS parser that incrementally processes arbitrary byte streams into a structured document model.</p>

4.04235 18.0962 4.40306 18.1289 4.80371C18.1657 5.25395 18.165 5.81091 18.165 6.5V9.33301Z"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-csharp"><span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">IEscPosParser</span></span><span>
{
    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Feed</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span></span><span>[] data);
    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Complete</span></span><span>();
    List&lt;Element&gt; Document { </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">get</span></span><span>; }
}
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="1722" data-end="2032"><strong data-start="1722" data-end="1738">Description:</strong><br data-start="1738" data-end="1741">
The parser accepts ESC/POS printer command data through the <code data-start="1803" data-end="1811">Feed()</code> method. Input data may arrive in arbitrary chunks, possibly split between command sequences. The parser must correctly handle incomplete data by maintaining internal state and buffering until a full command is available.</p>
<p data-start="2037" data-end="2178">As commands are recognized, they are converted into strongly typed <code data-start="2104" data-end="2113">Element</code> objects derived from the base class <code data-start="2150" data-end="2159">Element</code>. Examples include:</p>
<ul data-start="2181" data-end="2322">
<li data-start="2181" data-end="2196">
<p data-start="2183" data-end="2196"><code data-start="2183" data-end="2196">TextElement</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="2199" data-end="2217">
<p data-start="2201" data-end="2217"><code data-start="2201" data-end="2217">BarcodeElement</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="2220" data-end="2237">
<p data-start="2222" data-end="2237"><code data-start="2222" data-end="2237">QrcodeElement</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="2240" data-end="2262">
<p data-start="2242" data-end="2262"><code data-start="2242" data-end="2262">RasterImageElement</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="2265" data-end="2283">
<p data-start="2267" data-end="2283"><code data-start="2267" data-end="2283">PageCutElement</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="2286" data-end="2302">
<p data-start="2288" data-end="2302"><code data-start="2288" data-end="2302">PulseElement</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="2305" data-end="2320">
<p data-start="2307" data-end="2320"><code data-start="2307" data-end="2320">BellElement</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="2325" data-end="2421">Each element class encapsulates the commands parameters according to the ESC/POS specification.</p>
<p data-start="2426" data-end="2598">Instead of hardcoding command handling logic, the parser should use a declarative definition of supported commandsstored as a list of descriptors. Each descriptor defines:</p>
<ul data-start="2601" data-end="2747">
<li data-start="2601" data-end="2647">
<p data-start="2603" data-end="2647">The commands byte sequence (prefix/pattern)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2650" data-end="2675">
<p data-start="2652" data-end="2675">Its parameter structure</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2678" data-end="2745">
<p data-start="2680" data-end="2745">The function or factory that produces the corresponding <code data-start="2736" data-end="2745">Element</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="2750" data-end="2949"><strong data-start="2750" data-end="2764">Objective:</strong><br data-start="2764" data-end="2767">
Design an efficient and maintainable implementation of <code data-start="2824" data-end="2839">IEscPosParser</code> that separates protocol data definitions from parsing logic, allowing easy extension to new ESC/POS commands.</p>
</blockquote>
<hr data-start="2951" data-end="2954">
<p data-start="2956" data-end="3113" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">Would you like me next to propose the <strong data-start="2994" data-end="3045">structure of the declarative command definition</strong> (i.e., how to represent ESC/POS commands in data rather than code)?</p></div></div></div></div><div class="z-0 flex min-h-[46px] justify-start"><div class="touch:-me-2 extra constraints. Heres whats still unclear (so we dont trip later), plus a tightened task statement that reflects your rules.</p>

<h1 data-start="160" data-end="215">Whats still missing / ambiguous (after your updates)</h1>
<ol data-start="217" data-end="2732">
<li data-start="217" data-end="397">
<p data-start="220" data-end="251"><strong data-start="220" data-end="251">Coverage/version of ESC/POS</strong></p>
<ul data-start="255" data-end="397">
<li data-start="255" data-end="397">
<p data-start="257" data-end="397">Which spec/version(s) are you targeting as authoritative? (Different vendors extend thingshelps to lock to baseline + listed extensions.)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="399" data-end="715">
<p data-start="402" data-end="448"><strong data-start="402" data-end="448">Framing rules for variable-length commands</strong></p>
<ul data-start="452" data-end="715">
<li data-start="452" data-end="715">
<p data-start="454" data-end="715">For patterns like QR and raster (e.g., <code data-start="493" data-end="501">GS ( k</code>, <code data-start="503" data-end="511">GS v 0</code> / <code data-start="514" data-end="522">GS ( L</code>), confirm how length fields are interpreted (endianness, inclusivity), and how you want to treat partial payloads in the middle of a multi-part sequence (single <code data-start="684" data-end="700">UnknownElement</code> vs. multiple).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="717" data-end="1038">
<p data-start="720" data-end="748"><strong data-start="720" data-end="748">Resynchronization policy</strong></p>
<ul data-start="752" data-end="1038">
<li data-start="752" data-end="1038">
<p data-start="754" data-end="826">When a parse fails mid-command, how aggressively should we skip forward?</p>
<ul data-start="832" data-end="1038">
<li data-start="832" data-end="948">
<p data-start="834" data-end="948">Minimal skip (advance by 1 byte and retry) vs. skip to next plausible lead byte (<code data-start="915" data-end="920">ESC</code>, <code data-start="922" data-end="926">GS</code>, <code data-start="928" data-end="932">FS</code>, <code data-start="934" data-end="939">DLE</code>, <code data-start="941" data-end="946">BEL</code>).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="954" data-end="1038">
<p data-start="956" data-end="1038">On <code data-start="959" data-end="971">Complete()</code>, should any leftover bytes be emitted as a final <code data-start="1021" data-end="1037">UnknownElement</code>?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="1040" data-end="1296">
<p data-start="1043" data-end="1070"><strong data-start="1043" data-end="1070">Text segmentation rules</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1074" data-end="1296">
<li data-start="1074" data-end="1215">
<p data-start="1076" data-end="1099">What ends a <code data-start="1088" data-end="1098">TextLine</code>?</p>
<ul data-start="1105" data-end="1215">
<li data-start="1105" data-end="1126">
<p data-start="1107" data-end="1126">Newline bytes only?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1132" data-end="1215">
<p data-start="1134" data-end="1215">Mode changes (e.g., <code data-start="1154" data-end="1167">SetBoldMode</code>) cause a flush of the current <code data-start="1198" data-end="1208">TextLine</code> first?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="1219" data-end="1296">
<p data-start="1221" data-end="1296">Are multiple <code data-start="1234" data-end="1244">TextLine</code> elements allowed without explicit newline commands?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="1298" data-end="1726">
<p data-start="1301" data-end="1334"><strong data-start="1301" data-end="1334">Stateful feature interactions</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1338" data-end="1726">
<li data-start="1338" data-end="1587">
<p data-start="1340" data-end="1587">Some commands are split across multiple ops (e.g., QR: set model/size/EC  store data  print). Should we emit intermediate elements (e.g., <code data-start="1480" data-end="1493">StoreQrData</code>) as-is (as you listed), or aggregate them into one final <code data-start="1551" data-end="1564">PrintQrCode</code> element at print time?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1591" data-end="1726">
<p data-start="1593" data-end="1726">For raster: confirm whether <code data-start="1621" data-end="1644">RasterImageDescriptor</code> and <code data-start="1649" data-end="1669">RasterImageContent</code> are always adjacent and how to pair them if interleaved.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="1728" data-end="2084">
<p data-start="1731" data-end="1760"><strong data-start="1731" data-end="1760">Status/real-time commands</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1764" data-end="2084">
<li data-start="1764" data-end="2084">
<p data-start="1766" data-end="1931">You listed <code data-start="1777" data-end="1792">PrinterStatus</code> and <code data-start="1797" data-end="1811">PrinterError</code>. ESC/POS status is often a <em data-start="1839" data-end="1846">query</em> (<code data-start="1848" data-end="1859">DLE EOT n</code>, <code data-start="1861" data-end="1869">GS r n</code>) whose <em data-start="1877" data-end="1887">response</em> bytes come asynchronously. Are you parsing:</p>
<ul data-start="1937" data-end="2084">
<li data-start="1937" data-end="2084">
<p data-start="1939" data-end="2084">Only the bytes sent <em data-start="1959" data-end="1963">to</em> the printer, or also the status bytes <em data-start="2002" data-end="2008">from</em> the printer? (If both, well need channel/source tagging or a mode switch.)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="2086" data-end="2274">
<p data-start="2089" data-end="2122"><strong data-start="2089" data-end="2122">Error reporting / diagnostics</strong></p>
<ul data-start="2126" data-end="2274">
<li data-start="2126" data-end="2274">
<p data-start="2128" data-end="2274">Beyond emitting <code data-start="2144" data-end="2169">UnknownElement(rawData)</code>, do you want a side-channel for warnings (e.g., invalid barcode type value 0x07)? Logging hook? Stats?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="2276" data-end="2437">
<p data-start="2279" data-end="2302"><strong data-start="2279" data-end="2302">Performance targets</strong></p>
<ul data-start="2306" data-end="2437">
<li data-start="2306" data-end="2437">
<p data-start="2308" data-end="2437">Expected throughput, typical chunk sizes, max document length, and memory constraints (impacts buffer and backtracking strategy).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="2439" data-end="2704">
<p data-start="2442" data-end="2462"><strong data-start="2442" data-end="2462">Encoding details</strong></p>
<ul data-start="2466" data-end="2704">
<li data-start="2466" data-end="2613">
<p data-start="2468" data-end="2613">Mapping for <code data-start="2480" data-end="2493">SetCodePage</code> values to .NET encodings (some vendor IDs dont map 1:1; do you want best-effort fallback, or strict only-known sets?).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2617" data-end="2704">
<p data-start="2619" data-end="2704">Replacement behavior for undecodable bytes (throw, U+FFFD, or preserve raw escapes?).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="2706" data-end="2732">
<p data-start="2710" data-end="2732"><strong data-start="2710" data-end="2732">Document lifecycle</strong></p>
</li>
</ol>
<ul data-start="2736" data-end="2863">
<li data-start="2736" data-end="2778">
<p data-start="2738" data-end="2778">Is <code data-start="2741" data-end="2751">Document</code> append-only while parsing?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2782" data-end="2863">
<p data-start="2784" data-end="2863">Does <code data-start="2789" data-end="2801">Complete()</code> finalize and prevent further <code data-start="2831" data-end="2839">Feed()</code> calls, or can we reset?</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="2865" data-end="2868">
<h1 data-start="2870" data-end="2920">Rephrased task (with your constraints folded in)</h1>
<blockquote data-start="2922" data-end="4877">
<p data-start="2924" data-end="3091"><strong data-start="2924" data-end="2937">Objective</strong><br data-start="2937" data-end="2940">
Build an efficient, stateful ESC/POS stream parser that consumes arbitrarily chunked byte input and emits a structured sequence of document elements.</p>
<p data-start="3096" data-end="3111"><strong data-start="3096" data-end="3109">Interface</strong></p>

class="whitespace-pre! language-csharp"><span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">IEscPosParser</span></span><span>
{
    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Feed</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span></span><span>[] data);
    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Complete</span></span><span>();
    List&lt;Element&gt; Document { </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">get</span></span><span>; }
}
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="3259" data-end="3273"><strong data-start="3259" data-end="3271">Behavior</strong></p>
<ul data-start="3276" data-end="4490">
<li data-start="3276" data-end="3393">
<p data-start="3278" data-end="3393">The parser accepts byte chunks via <code data-start="3313" data-end="3321">Feed()</code>; commands may be split across chunk boundaries with arbitrary delays.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3396" data-end="3505">
<p data-start="3398" data-end="3505">It maintains internal state (e.g., current code page, text modes, barcode/QR configuration) across calls.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3508" data-end="4093">
<p data-start="3510" data-end="3585">When a complete command is recognized, it emits a strongly-typed <code data-start="3575" data-end="3584">Element</code>:</p>
<ul data-start="3590" data-end="4093">
<li data-start="3590" data-end="4093">
<p data-start="3592" data-end="4093"><code data-start="3592" data-end="3602">TextLine</code>, <code data-start="3604" data-end="3618">PrintBarcode</code>, <code data-start="3620" data-end="3633">PrintQrCode</code>, <code data-start="3635" data-end="3658">RasterImageDescriptor</code>, <code data-start="3660" data-end="3680">RasterImageContent</code>, <code data-start="3682" data-end="3694">StoredLogo</code>, <code data-start="3696" data-end="3705">Pagecut</code>, <code data-start="3707" data-end="3714">Pulse</code>, <code data-start="3716" data-end="3722">Bell</code>, <code data-start="3724" data-end="3738">ResetPrinter</code>, plus mode/state setters like <code data-start="3769" data-end="3778">SetFont</code>, <code data-start="3780" data-end="3793" data-is-only-node="">SetBoldMode</code>, <code data-start="3795" data-end="3813">SetUnderlineMode</code>, <code data-start="3815" data-end="3833">SetJustification</code>, <code data-start="3835" data-end="3851">SetLineSpacing</code>/<code data-start="3852" data-end="3870">ResetLineSpacing</code>, <code data-start="3872" data-end="3885">SetCodePage</code>, <code data-start="3887" data-end="3905">SetBarcodeHeight</code>, <code data-start="3907" data-end="3932">SetBarcodeLabelPosition</code>, <code data-start="3934" data-end="3957">SetBarcodeModuleWidth</code>, <code data-start="3959" data-end="3971">SetQrModel</code>, <code data-start="3973" data-end="3990">SetQrModuleSize</code>, <code data-start="3992" data-end="4014">SetQrErrorCorrection</code>, and status elements <code data-start="4036" data-end="4051">PrinterStatus</code>, <code data-start="4053" data-end="4067">PrinterError</code>, <code data-start="4069" data-end="4076">Error</code> (per your list).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="4096" data-end="4295">
<p data-start="4098" data-end="4295">Text bytes are preserved and decoded into UTF-8 strings in <code data-start="4157" data-end="4167">TextLine</code> using the current ESC/POS code page (set via <code data-start="4213" data-end="4226">SetCodePage</code>); raw bytes must be accepted, then decoded using the active mapping.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="4298" data-end="4449">
<p data-start="4300" data-end="4449">Incomplete or malformed sequences must produce <code data-start="4347" data-end="4379">UnknownElement(byte[] rawData)</code> while attempting to resynchronize to the next valid command boundary.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="4452" data-end="4488">
<p data-start="4454" data-end="4488">Thread-safety is <strong data-start="4471" data-end="4478">not</strong> required.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="4493" data-end="4511"><strong data-start="4493" data-end="4509">Design goals</strong></p>
<ul data-start="4514" data-end="4877">
<li data-start="4514" data-end="4672">
<p data-start="4516" data-end="4672">Separate protocol data from parsing logic: define supported commands declaratively (a list of command descriptors) instead of hardcoding switch/if chains.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="4675" data-end="4769">
<p data-start="4677" data-end="4769">Efficient streaming: incremental parsing with bounded buffering and fast resync on errors.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="4772" data-end="4877">
<p data-start="4774" data-end="4877">Extensibility: adding a new ESC/POS command requires adding a descriptor, not changing the core parser.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
<hr data-start="4879" data-end="4882">
<h2 data-start="4884" data-end="4944">Suggested next step (so we can move forward productively)</h2>
<p data-start="4946" data-end="5232">If youre good with the above, Ill propose a concrete <strong data-start="5001" data-end="5022">descriptor schema</strong> and the <strong data-start="5031" data-end="5051">core parser loop</strong> (including buffering and resynchronization), with 34 worked examples (e.g., <code data-start="5129" data-end="5134">BEL</code>, <code data-start="5136" data-end="5143">ESC @</code>, <code data-start="5145" data-end="5154">ESC t n</code>, <code data-start="5156" data-end="5164">GS V m</code> page cut, <code data-start="5175" data-end="5183">GS ( k</code> QR store/print) that match your element types.</p>

class="min-h-8 text-message relative flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 text-start break-words whitespace-normal [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-1" data-message-model-slug="gpt-5-thinking"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[1px]"><div class="markdown prose dark:prose-invert w-full break-words light markdown-new-styling"><p data-start="0" data-end="348">Great  thanks, that nails down the policy. Below is a concrete design you can implement right away: a <strong data-start="103" data-end="131">descriptor-driven parser</strong> with a small <strong data-start="145" data-end="160">opcode trie</strong>, a clean <strong data-start="170" data-end="189">resync strategy</strong>, and a few <strong data-start="201" data-end="228">worked command examples</strong> (BEL, ESC @, ESC t n, GS V cuts, QR GS ( k). Im keeping the code focused so you can drop it into a project and extend.</p>
<hr data-start="350" data-end="353">
<h1 data-start="355" data-end="383">Agreed constraints (short)</h1>
<ul data-start="385" data-end="1204">
<li data-start="385" data-end="413">
<p data-start="387" data-end="413"><strong data-start="387" data-end="413">Baseline ESC/POS only.</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="414" data-end="540">
<p data-start="416" data-end="540"><strong data-start="416" data-end="443">Variable-length framing</strong>: obey spec; if a known command is <em data-start="478" data-end="499">possibly incomplete</em>, <strong data-start="501" data-end="509">wait</strong> (dont emit <code data-start="522" data-end="538">UnknownElement</code>).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="541" data-end="779">
<p data-start="543" data-end="561"><strong data-start="543" data-end="560">Unknown bytes</strong>:</p>
<ul data-start="564" data-end="779">
<li data-start="564" data-end="688">
<p data-start="566" data-end="688">While streaming: only emit <code data-start="593" data-end="609">UnknownElement</code> if were sure bytes cannot be part of any known command and are not printable.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="691" data-end="779">
<p data-start="693" data-end="779">On <code data-start="696" data-end="708">Complete()</code>: emit any <strong data-start="719" data-end="731">leftover</strong> unrecognized bytes as a final <code data-start="762" data-end="778">UnknownElement</code>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="780" data-end="898">
<p data-start="782" data-end="898"><strong data-start="782" data-end="797">Granularity</strong>: emit <strong data-start="804" data-end="811">all</strong> intermediate commands (dont aggregate QR steps, raster descriptors vs content, etc.).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="899" data-end="977">
<p data-start="901" data-end="977"><strong data-start="901" data-end="919">Status queries</strong>: parse the <em data-start="931" data-end="938">query</em> bytes only (caller handles responses).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="978" data-end="1010">
<p data-start="980" data-end="1010"><strong data-start="980" data-end="1000">No thread safety</strong> required.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1011" data-end="1149">
<p data-start="1013" data-end="1149"><strong data-start="1013" data-end="1027">Code pages</strong>: start with a small set (e.g., 437, 866, 850, 1251), and decode text into UTF-8 in <code data-start="1112" data-end="1122">TextLine</code> according to current page.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1150" data-end="1204">
<p data-start="1152" data-end="1204"><strong data-start="1152" data-end="1166">Complete()</strong> finalizes; later <code data-start="1184" data-end="1192">Feed()</code> is a no-op.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1206" data-end="1209">
<h1 data-start="1211" data-end="1230">Core architecture</h1>
<h2 data-start="1232" data-end="1255">1) Descriptor schema</h2>
<p data-start="1257" data-end="1306">A descriptor is a small object that knows how to:</p>
<ul data-start="1307" data-end="1422">
<li data-start="1307" data-end="1336">
<p data-start="1309" data-end="1336">recognize a command prefix,</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1337" data-end="1376">
<p data-start="1339" data-end="1376">decide if enough bytes are available,</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1377" data-end="1400">
<p data-start="1379" data-end="1400">compute total length,</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1401" data-end="1422">
<p data-start="1403" data-end="1422">build an <code data-start="1412" data-end="1421">Element</code>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<pre class="overflow-visible!" data-start="1424" data-end="2306"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl">csharp</div><div class="sticky top-9"><div class="absolute end-0 class="whitespace-pre! language-csharp"><span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">sealed</span></span><span> </span><span><span {
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span> CurrentCodePageId { </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">get</span></span><span>; </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">set</span></span><span>; } = </span><span><span class="hljs-number">437</span></span><span>; </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// default</span></span><span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">bool</span></span><span> Bold { </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">get</span></span><span>; </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">set</span></span><span>; }
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">bool</span></span><span> Underline { </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">get</span></span><span>; </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">set</span></span><span>; }
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span><span> Justification { </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">get</span></span><span>; </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">set</span></span><span>; } </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// 0,1,2</span></span><span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span><span> Font { </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">get</span></span><span>; </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">set</span></span><span>; } </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// baseline A/B, etc.</span></span><span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Add barcode/QR settings as needed.</span></span><span>

    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Text buffer accumulates raw bytes between control ops / LFs.</span></span><span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span><span> List&lt;</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span><span>&gt; TextBuffer { </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">get</span></span><span>; } = </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span>();

</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<h2 data-start="3649" data-end="3694">3) IEscPosParser implementation (skeleton)</h2>
<ul data-start="3696" data-end="4150">
<li data-start="3696" data-end="3780">
<p data-start="3698" data-end="3780"><strong data-start="3698" data-end="3711">Buffering</strong>: keep an internal <code data-start="3730" data-end="3742">List&lt;byte&gt;</code> (or <code data-start="3747" data-end="3760">ArrayBuffer</code>) with a read index.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3781" data-end="3879">
<p data-start="3783" data-end="3879"><strong data-start="3783" data-end="3795">Dispatch</strong>: dictionary from <code data-start="3813" data-end="3823">LeadByte</code>  list of <code data-start="3834" data-end="3847">ICommandDef</code> ordered by most-specific first.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3880" data-end="4150">
<p data-start="3882" data-end="3891"><strong data-start="3882" data-end="3890">Loop</strong>:</p>
<ol data-start="3894" data-end="4150">
<li data-start="3894" data-end="3987">
<p data-start="3897" data-end="3987">If printable at head, accumulate into <code data-start="3935" data-end="3947">TextBuffer</code> and advance until a control lead or LF.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3990" data-end="4036">
<p data-start="3993" data-end="4036">Otherwise, try command defs for <code data-start="4025" data-end="4035">LeadByte</code>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="4039" data-end="4150">
<p data-start="4042" data-end="4150">If all return <code data-start="4056" data-end="4065">NoMatch</code>, start/extend an <code data-start="4083" data-end="4092">Unknown</code> run until next plausible lead byte or printable sequence.</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="4152" data-end="4173">Pseudocode (real C#):</p>

class="whitespace-pre! language-csharp"><span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">sealed</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">EscPosParser</span></span><span> : </span><span><span class="hljs-title">IEscPosParser</span></span><span>
{
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">readonly</span></span><span> Dictionary&lt;</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span><span>, List&lt;ICommandDef&gt;&gt; _defs;
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">readonly</span></span><span> List&lt;Element&gt; _doc = </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span>();
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">readonly</span></span><span> List&lt;</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span><span>&gt; _buf = </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span>(); </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// rolling buffer</span></span><span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span> _read;
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">bool</span></span><span> _finalized;
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">readonly</span></span><span> ParserState _state = </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span>();
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">readonly</span></span><span> EncodingSelector _enc = </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span>();

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span><span> List&lt;Element&gt; Document =&gt; _doc;

    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">EscPosParser</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">IEnumerable&lt;ICommandDef&gt; defs</span></span><span>)
    {
        _defs = defs.GroupBy(d =&gt; d.LeadByte)
                    .ToDictionary(g =&gt; g.Key, g =&gt; g.OrderByDescending(Specificity).ToList());
        </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">static</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Specificity</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">ICommandDef d</span></span><span>) =&gt; d </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">is</span></span><span> FixedPrefixCommand f ? f.GetType().Name.Length : </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>; </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// cheap tie-break</span></span><span>
    }

    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Feed</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span></span><span>[] data)
    {
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (_finalized || data </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">is</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">null</span></span><span> || data.Length == </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span>;
        _buf.AddRange(data);
        Parse();
    }

    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Complete</span></span><span>()
    {
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (_finalized) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span>;
        </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Flush any pending text line</span></span><span>
        FlushTextLineIfAny();
        </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Emit leftover as UnknownElement</span></span><span>
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (_read &lt; _buf.Count)
        {
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span></span><span> raw = _buf.Skip(_read).ToArray();
            _doc.Add(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> UnknownElement(raw));
        }
        _finalized = </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">true</span></span><span>;
    }

    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Parse</span></span><span>()
    {
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">while</span></span><span> (_read &lt; _buf.Count)
        {
            </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span><span> b = _buf[_read];

            </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Fast path: printable stream (text)</span></span><span>
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (Bytes.IsPrintable(b))
            {
                ConsumePrintableRun();
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span></span><span>;
            }

            </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Line feed -&gt; end of text line</span></span><span>
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (b == </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0x0A</span></span><span>) { _read++; FlushTextLineIfAny(); </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span></span><span>; }

            </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Try command defs</span></span><span>
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (_defs.TryGetValue(b, </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">out</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span></span><span> list))
            {
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span></span><span> span = CollectionsMarshal.AsSpan(_buf).Slice(_read);
                MatchResult best = MatchResult.NoMatch();
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">foreach</span></span><span> (</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span></span><span> def </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> list)
                {
                    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span></span><span> mr = def.TryMatch(span, _state);
                    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (mr.Kind == MatchKind.Matched)
                    {
                        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (mr.Element </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">is</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">not</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">null</span></span><span>)
                        {
                            </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Before control element, close any open text</span></span><span>
                            FlushTextLineIfAny();
                            _doc.Add(mr.Element);
                        }
                        _read += mr.BytesConsumed;
                        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span></span><span> next;
                    }
                    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (mr.Kind == MatchKind.NeedMore) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span>; </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// wait for more bytes</span></span><span>
                }
                </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// No descriptor matched: treat as unknown/control; collect until next plausible boundary</span></span><span>
                ConsumeUnknownRun();
                next: </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span></span><span>;
            }
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>
            {
                </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Not a known lead byte: either control garbage or extended printable</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (Bytes.IsPrintable(b)) { ConsumePrintableRun(); }
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span> { ConsumeUnknownRun(); }
            }
        }
    }

    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">ConsumePrintableRun</span></span><span>()
    {
        </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span> i = _read;
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">while</span></span><span> (i &lt; _buf.Count &amp;&amp; Bytes.IsPrintable(_buf[i])) i++;
        _state.TextBuffer.AddRange(_buf.Skip(_read).Take(i - _read));
        _read = i;
    }

    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">FlushTextLineIfAny</span></span><span>()
    {
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (_state.TextBuffer.Count == </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span>;
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span></span><span> bytes = CollectionsMarshal.AsSpan(_state.TextBuffer).ToArray();
        _state.TextBuffer.Clear();
        </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span><span> text = _enc.Decode(_state.CurrentCodePageId, bytes);
        _doc.Add(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> TextLine { Text = text }); </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// add any style snapshot if you track it</span></span><span>
    }

    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Resync policy: advance until a plausible lead (ESC 1B, GS 1D, FS 1C, DLE 10, BEL 07, LF 0A) or printable</span></span><span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">static</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">readonly</span></span><span> HashSet&lt;</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span><span>&gt; Leads = </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span>([</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0x1B</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0x1D</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0x1C</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0x10</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0x07</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0x0A</span></span><span>]);
    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">private</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">ConsumeUnknownRun</span></span><span>()
    {
        </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span> i = _read;
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">while</span></span><span> (i &lt; _buf.Count)
        {
            </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span><span> b = _buf[i];
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (Bytes.IsPrintable(b) || Leads.Contains(b)) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">break</span></span><span>;
            i++;
        }
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (i &gt; _read)
        {
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span></span><span> raw = _buf.Skip(_read).Take(i - _read).ToArray();
            _doc.Add(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> UnknownElement(raw));
            _read = i;
        }
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>
        {
            </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// single stray control byte; treat as unknown and step</span></span><span>
            _doc.Add(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> UnknownElement(</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span>[] { _buf[_read] }));
            _read++;
        }
    }
}
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<blockquote data-start="8657" data-end="8822">
<p data-start="8659" data-end="8822">Note: <code data-start="8665" data-end="8674">Parse()</code> <strong data-start="8675" data-end="8684">never</strong> emits <code data-start="8691" data-end="8707">UnknownElement</code> for a <em data-start="8714" data-end="8752">potentially incomplete known command</em>those return <code data-start="8766" data-end="8776">NeedMore</code> and the loop exits to await further <code data-start="8813" data-end="8821">Feed()</code>.</p>
</blockquote>

    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">string</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Decode</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span></span><span> page, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span><span>[] bytes)

<hr data-start="9671" data-end="9674">
<h1 data-start="9676" data-end="9704">Worked command descriptors</h1>
<p data-start="9706" data-end="9770">Below are concise descriptors you can copy/extend. Each returns:</p>
<ul data-start="9771" data-end="9892">
<li data-start="9771" data-end="9823">
<p data-start="9773" data-end="9823"><code data-start="9773" data-end="9783">NeedMore</code> if prefix matches but frame incomplete.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="9824" data-end="9869">
<p data-start="9826" data-end="9869"><code data-start="9826" data-end="9854">Matched(consumed, element)</code> when complete.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="9870" data-end="9892">
<p data-start="9872" data-end="9892"><code data-start="9872" data-end="9881">NoMatch</code> otherwise.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="9894" data-end="9917">BEL (0x07)  <code data-start="9911" data-end="9917">Bell</code></h3>
<pre class="overflow-visible!" data-start="9919" data-end="10183"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl">csharp</div><div class="sticky top-9"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path d="M12.668 10.667C12.668 <h3 data-start="11665" data-end="11695">GS V m  (Cut)  <code data-start="11686" data-end="11695">Pagecut</code></h3>
<p data-start="11697" data-end="11715">Baseline variants:</p>
<ul data-start="11716" data-end="11799">
<li data-start="11716" data-end="11738">
<p data-start="11718" data-end="11738"><code data-start="11718" data-end="11726">GS V 0</code> (full cut),</p>
</li>
<li data-start="11739" data-end="11760">
<p data-start="11741" data-end="11760"><code data-start="11741" data-end="11749">GS V 1</code> (partial),</p>
</li>
<li data-start="11761" data-end="11799">
<p data-start="11763" data-end="11799"><code data-start="11763" data-end="11774">GS V 66 n</code> (feed n lines then cut).</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 data-start="12680" data-end="12751">QR: GS ( k pL pH cn fn   <code data-start="12711" data-end="12724">StoreQrData</code> / <code data-start="12727" data-end="12740">PrintQrCode</code> / settings</h3>
<p data-start="12753" data-end="12770">Baseline framing:</p>
<ul data-start="12771" data-end="13093">
<li data-start="12771" data-end="12800">
<p data-start="12773" data-end="12800"><code data-start="12773" data-end="12781">GS ( k</code> (0x1D, 0x28, 0x6B)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="12801" data-end="12890">
<p data-start="12803" data-end="12890">next 2 bytes: length L = pL | pH&lt;&lt;8 (LE), <strong data-start="12845" data-end="12874">number of bytes following</strong> (cn, fn, data)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="12891" data-end="12904">
<p data-start="12893" data-end="12904"><code data-start="12893" data-end="12897">cn</code> = 0x31</p>
</li>
<li data-start="12905" data-end="13093">
<p data-start="12907" data-end="12919"><code data-start="12907" data-end="12911">fn</code> varies:</p>
<ul data-start="12922" data-end="13093">
<li data-start="12922" data-end="12956">
<p data-start="12924" data-end="12956"><code data-start="12924" data-end="12930">0x43</code> set module size (1 byte),</p>
</li>
<li data-start="12959" data-end="13018">
<p data-start="12961" data-end="13018"><code data-start="12961" data-end="12967">0x45</code> set error correction (1 byte, 48..51 for L/M/Q/H),</p>
</li>
<li data-start="13021" data-end="13065">
<p data-start="13023" data-end="13065"><code data-start="13023" data-end="13029">0x50</code> store data: <code data-start="13042" data-end="13050">m=0x30</code>, then payload,</p>
</li>
<li data-start="13068" data-end="13093">
<p data-start="13070" data-end="13093"><code data-start="13070" data-end="13076">0x51</code> print: <code data-start="13084" data-end="13092">m=0x30</code>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="13095" data-end="13131">We emit <strong data-start="13103" data-end="13111">each</strong> as its own element.</p>

<h3 data-start="14682" data-end="14765">Raster: GS v 0 m xL xH yL yH   <code data-start="14719" data-end="14742">RasterImageDescriptor</code> + <code data-start="14745" data-end="14765">RasterImageContent</code></h3>
<p data-start="14767" data-end="15049">You said you want <strong data-start="14785" data-end="14793">both</strong> descriptor and content elements. Define one descriptor that parses the header and one content command that expects exactly <code data-start="14917" data-end="14933">xBytes * yRows</code> of raster payload (or, for the (L variants, use length framing). For brevity, heres the classic <code data-start="15033" data-end="15041">GS v 0</code> header:</p>

</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="15791" data-end="16106">Then a <strong data-start="15798" data-end="15809">content</strong> def that consumes the exact payload bytes (registered under the any lead bucket, but activated only if weve just seen a descriptor). Easiest: maintain a <code data-start="15966" data-end="15981">PendingRaster</code> counter in <code data-start="15993" data-end="16006">ParserState</code> with remaining size, and a single content pseudo-descriptor that fires while <code data-start="16086" data-end="16105">PendingRaster &gt; 0</code>.</p>
<hr data-start="16108" data-end="16111">

{
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> BellDef(),
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> ResetDef(),
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> SetCodePageDef(),
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> CutDef(),
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> QrDef(),
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> RasterHeaderDef(),
    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// plus SetBold, SetUnderline, SetFont, SetJustification, SetLineSpacing/ResetLineSpacing,</span></span><span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment">// Barcode setters &amp; print, StoredLogo, Pulse, PrinterStatus/PrinterError, etc.</span></span><span>
};

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span></span><span> parser = </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">new</span></span><span> EscPosParser(defs);
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="16531" data-end="16534">
<h1 data-start="16536" data-end="16574">Text handling: like a real printer</h1>
<ul data-start="16576" data-end="17113">
<li data-start="16576" data-end="16679">
<p data-start="16578" data-end="16679">Treat any <strong data-start="16588" data-end="16601">printable</strong> bytes (0x20..0x7E and 0x80..0xFF) as text stream under the current code page.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="16680" data-end="16751">
<p data-start="16682" data-end="16751"><strong data-start="16682" data-end="16695">LF (0x0A)</strong> ends the current text line  emit <code data-start="16730" data-end="16740">TextLine</code> (decoded).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="16752" data-end="16989">
<p data-start="16754" data-end="16989">Non-text commands (e.g., style changes) <strong data-start="16794" data-end="16804">do not</strong> force a newline; they <em data-start="16827" data-end="16831">do</em> cause a <strong data-start="16840" data-end="16849">flush</strong> of any currently buffered text <strong data-start="16881" data-end="16891">before</strong> emitting the control element, so style changes dont retroactively apply to already emitted text.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="16990" data-end="17113">
<p data-start="16992" data-end="17113"><code data-start="16992" data-end="17003">CR (0x0D)</code> can be ignored or handled as carriage return; baseline receipts are fine treating <code data-start="17086" data-end="17090">LF</code> as the line delimiter.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="17115" data-end="17233">You can refine this later (e.g., <code data-start="17148" data-end="17157">ESC d n</code>, <code data-start="17159" data-end="17166">ESC 2</code>, <code data-start="17168" data-end="17177">ESC 3 n</code> affecting line spacing) without changing the core loop.</p>
<hr data-start="17235" data-end="17238">
<h1 data-start="17240" data-end="17266">Resynchronization policy</h1>
<ul data-start="17268" data-end="18006">
<li data-start="17268" data-end="17353">
<p data-start="17270" data-end="17353"><strong data-start="17270" data-end="17289">Plausible leads</strong>: <code data-start="17291" data-end="17352">{ ESC 0x1B, GS 0x1D, FS 0x1C, DLE 0x10, BEL 0x07, LF 0x0A }</code>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="17354" data-end="17755">
<p data-start="17356" data-end="17532">When a byte isnt printable and <strong data-start="17388" data-end="17405">no descriptor</strong> matches its lead (and its not the start of a potentially incomplete known command), accumulate into an <strong data-start="17510" data-end="17525">Unknown run</strong> until:</p>
<ul data-start="17535" data-end="17755">
<li data-start="17535" data-end="17565">
<p data-start="17537" data-end="17565">you hit a printable byte, or</p>
</li>
<li data-start="17568" data-end="17755">
<p data-start="17570" data-end="17755">a plausible lead byte,<br>
then emit one <code data-start="17607" data-end="17623">UnknownElement</code> for that run. This naturally produces <strong data-start="17662" data-end="17692">multiple unknowns in a row</strong> if the garbage is interleaved with known leads (as requested).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="17757" data-end="18006">
<p data-start="17759" data-end="18006">On <code data-start="17762" data-end="17774">Complete()</code>, <strong data-start="17776" data-end="17793">any remaining</strong> bytes (even if printable text is partially buffered) are emitted as a final <code data-start="17870" data-end="17886">UnknownElement</code> (you said leftover <em data-start="17906" data-end="17920">unrecognized</em> bytes; if you prefer to flush partial text instead, we can flip that  just tell me).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="18008" data-end="18011">
<h1 data-start="18013" data-end="18024">Next step</h1>
<p data-start="18026" data-end="18063">If this structure looks right, I can:</p>
<ul data-start="18064" data-end="18387">
<li data-start="18064" data-end="18196">
<p data-start="18066" data-end="18196">add <strong data-start="18070" data-end="18094">34 more descriptors</strong> you listed (bold/underline/font/justification; barcode print and height/width/label position; pulse),</p>
</li>
<li data-start="18197" data-end="18263">
<p data-start="18199" data-end="18263">include a minimal <strong data-start="18217" data-end="18234">RasterContent</strong> pending-size implementation,</p>
</li>
<li data-start="18264" data-end="18387">
<p data-start="18266" data-end="18387">and provide <strong data-start="18278" data-end="18303">unit test scaffolding</strong> with byte sequences  element lists (including split-chunk tests and resync tests).</p>
</li>
</ul>

break-words whitespace-normal [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-1" data-message-model-slug="gpt-5"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[1px]"><div class="markdown prose dark:prose-invert w-full break-words light markdown-new-styling"><p data-start="0" data-end="194">Perfect  heres a <strong data-start="19" data-end="53">formal technical specification</strong> for your ESC/POS stream parser, written as a requirements document (no implementation details, just behavior, constraints, and structure).</p>
<hr data-start="196" data-end="199">
<h1 data-start="201" data-end="242"><strong data-start="203" data-end="242">ESC/POS Stream Parser Specification</strong></h1>
<h2 data-start="244" data-end="258">1. Overview</h2>
<p data-start="260" data-end="463">The ESC/POS parser is a <strong data-start="284" data-end="313">stateful stream processor</strong> that incrementally consumes arbitrary byte sequences representing ESC/POS printer data and produces a sequence of structured <strong data-start="439" data-end="460">document elements</strong>.</p>
<p data-start="465" data-end="687">It operates over <strong data-start="482" data-end="499">chunked input</strong>, where command sequences may arrive split across multiple <code data-start="558" data-end="566">Feed()</code> calls.<br data-start="573" data-end="576">
The parser maintains internal state to interpret context-dependent commands and emit meaningful typed elements.</p>
<hr data-start="689" data-end="692">
<h2 data-start="694" data-end="720">2. Interface Definition</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible!" data-start="722" data-end="848"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center {
    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Feed</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">byte</span></span></span><span>[] data);
    </span><span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span></span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title">Complete</span></span><span>();
    List&lt;Element&gt; Document { </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">get</span></span><span>; }
}
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<h3 data-start="850" data-end="877">2.1 <code data-start="858" data-end="877">Feed(byte[] data)</code></h3>
<ul data-start="878" data-end="1096">
<li data-start="878" data-end="916">
<p data-start="880" data-end="916">Accepts a new chunk of ESC/POS data.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="917" data-end="984">
<p data-start="919" data-end="984">Data may contain complete, partial, or multiple ESC/POS commands.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="985" data-end="1096">
<p data-start="987" data-end="1096">The parser must buffer incomplete sequences until sufficient bytes are available to recognize a full command.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="1098" data-end="1118">2.2 <code data-start="1106" data-end="1118">Complete()</code></h3>
<ul data-start="1119" data-end="1375">
<li data-start="1119" data-end="1159">
<p data-start="1121" data-end="1159">Signals that no more data will be fed.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1160" data-end="1375">
<p data-start="1162" data-end="1206">The parser finalizes its internal state and:</p>
<ul data-start="1209" data-end="1375">
<li data-start="1209" data-end="1237">
<p data-start="1211" data-end="1237">flushes any buffered text,</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1240" data-end="1313">
<p data-start="1242" data-end="1313">emits any remaining <strong data-start="1262" data-end="1284">unrecognized bytes</strong> as a final <code data-start="1296" data-end="1312">UnknownElement</code>,</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1316" data-end="1375">
<p data-start="1318" data-end="1375">prevents any further <code data-start="1339" data-end="1347">Feed()</code> calls (they become no-ops).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="1377" data-end="1395">2.3 <code data-start="1385" data-end="1395">Document</code></h3>
<ul data-start="1396" data-end="1557">
<li data-start="1396" data-end="1498">
<p data-start="1398" data-end="1498">Contains a sequential list of parsed <strong data-start="1435" data-end="1447">elements</strong> representing recognized ESC/POS commands and text.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1499" data-end="1557">
<p data-start="1501" data-end="1557">Order reflects the order of commands in the byte stream.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1559" data-end="1562">
<h2 data-start="1564" data-end="1583">3. Parsing Model</h2>
<h3 data-start="1585" data-end="1615">3.1 Incremental Processing</h3>
<ul data-start="1616" data-end="1855">
<li data-start="1616" data-end="1683">
<p data-start="1618" data-end="1683">The parser processes bytes sequentially as they become available.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1684" data-end="1743">
<p data-start="1686" data-end="1743">Commands may be <strong data-start="1702" data-end="1711">split</strong> across multiple <code data-start="1728" data-end="1736">Feed()</code> calls.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1744" data-end="1855">
<p data-start="1746" data-end="1855">If the current buffer ends in the middle of a known command, parsing pauses and resumes on the next <code data-start="1846" data-end="1854">Feed()</code>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="1857" data-end="1885">3.2 Recognition Strategy</h3>
<ul data-start="1886" data-end="2329">
<li data-start="1886" data-end="1991">
<p data-start="1888" data-end="1991">Commands are recognized using a <strong data-start="1920" data-end="1959">declarative command definition list</strong>, not hardcoded branching logic.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1992" data-end="2205">
<p data-start="1994" data-end="2028">Each command definition specifies:</p>
<ul data-start="2031" data-end="2205">
<li data-start="2031" data-end="2071">
<p data-start="2033" data-end="2071"><strong data-start="2033" data-end="2049">Prefix bytes</strong> or signature pattern.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2074" data-end="2136">
<p data-start="2076" data-end="2136"><strong data-start="2076" data-end="2105">Length determination rule</strong> (fixed or length-field-based).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2139" data-end="2205">
<p data-start="2141" data-end="2205"><strong data-start="2141" data-end="2161">Semantic mapping</strong> (which element to emit and its parameters).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="2206" data-end="2329">
<p data-start="2208" data-end="2329">Recognition is deterministic and leftmost-greedy: the longest valid command starting at the current position is selected.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="2331" data-end="2352">3.3 Text Handling</h3>
<ul data-start="2353" data-end="2740">
<li data-start="2353" data-end="2465">
<p data-start="2355" data-end="2465">Bytes not part of any control sequence and within printable ranges (0x200x7E, 0x800xFF) are treated as text.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2466" data-end="2554">
<p data-start="2468" data-end="2554">Consecutive printable bytes form a text segment accumulated into a <code data-start="2535" data-end="2545">TextLine</code> element.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2555" data-end="2653">
<p data-start="2557" data-end="2653">A <strong data-start="2559" data-end="2579">line feed (0x0A)</strong> ends the current text line and triggers emission of a <code data-start="2634" data-end="2644">TextLine</code> element.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2654" data-end="2740">
<p data-start="2656" data-end="2740">Any control command flushes the currently buffered text before emitting its element.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="2742" data-end="2762">3.4 Unknown Data</h3>
<ul data-start="2763" data-end="3241">
<li data-start="2763" data-end="2878">
<p data-start="2765" data-end="2878">If bytes cannot be matched to any known command and are not printable, they are grouped into an <code data-start="2861" data-end="2877">UnknownElement</code>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2879" data-end="3002">
<p data-start="2881" data-end="3002"><strong data-start="2881" data-end="2926">Multiple consecutive unrecognized regions</strong> result in multiple <code data-start="2946" data-end="2962">UnknownElement</code> instances, preserving stream structure.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3003" data-end="3148">
<p data-start="3005" data-end="3148">During incremental parsing, unrecognized bytes are not immediately emitted if they might still complete a valid command once more data arrives.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3149" data-end="3241">
<p data-start="3151" data-end="3241">On <code data-start="3154" data-end="3166">Complete()</code>, any remaining unrecognized bytes are emitted as a final <code data-start="3224" data-end="3240">UnknownElement</code>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="3243" data-end="3268">3.5 Resynchronization</h3>
<ul data-start="3269" data-end="3543">
<li data-start="3269" data-end="3411">
<p data-start="3271" data-end="3411">After encountering unrecognized data, the parser must attempt to <strong data-start="3336" data-end="3353">resynchronize</strong> by scanning forward to the next plausible command prefix.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3412" data-end="3543">
<p data-start="3414" data-end="3543">Plausible leads include common control characters:<br data-start="3464" data-end="3467">
<code data-start="3469" data-end="3542">{ 0x1B (ESC), 0x1D (GS), 0x1C (FS), 0x10 (DLE), 0x07 (BEL), 0x0A (LF) }</code>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="3545" data-end="3548">
<h2 data-start="3550" data-end="3568">4. Parser State</h2>
<p data-start="3570" data-end="3650">The parser maintains contextual state required to interpret subsequent commands.</p>

<p data-start="4257" data-end="4354">State changes are applied when relevant commands are recognized and emitted as separate elements.</p>
<hr data-start="4356" data-end="4359">
<h2 data-start="4361" data-end="4390">5. Supported Element Types</h2>
<p data-start="4392" data-end="4460">Each recognized command produces one of the following element types:</p>

<p data-start="5218" data-end="5285">All listed element types are derived from the base class <code data-start="5275" data-end="5284">Element</code>.</p>
<hr data-start="5287" data-end="5290">
<h2 data-start="5292" data-end="5311">6. Text Encoding</h2>
<ul data-start="5313" data-end="5769">
<li data-start="5313" data-end="5382">
<p data-start="5315" data-end="5382">ESC/POS text bytes are decoded to UTF-8 using the active code page.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="5383" data-end="5467">
<p data-start="5385" data-end="5467">The active code page is changed via the <code data-start="5425" data-end="5434">ESC t n</code> command (<code data-start="5444" data-end="5457">SetCodePage</code> element).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="5468" data-end="5639">
<p data-start="5470" data-end="5536">The parser supports a <strong data-start="5492" data-end="5529">limited set of initial code pages</strong>, e.g.:</p>
<ul data-start="5539" data-end="5639">
<li data-start="5539" data-end="5566">
<p data-start="5541" data-end="5566">437 (USA/Standard Europe)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="5569" data-end="5589">
<p data-start="5571" data-end="5589">850 (Multilingual)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="5592" data-end="5611">
<p data-start="5594" data-end="5611">866 (Cyrillic #2)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="5614" data-end="5639">
<p data-start="5616" data-end="5639">1251 (Windows Cyrillic)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="5640" data-end="5706">
<p data-start="5642" data-end="5706">Unsupported selectors map to a default fallback (typically 437).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="5707" data-end="5769">
<p data-start="5709" data-end="5769">Decoding uses best-effort replacement for undecodable bytes.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="5771" data-end="5774">
<h2 data-start="5776" data-end="5803">7. Command Parsing Rules</h2>
<h3 data-start="5805" data-end="5840">7.1 General Command Recognition</h3>
<ul data-start="5841" data-end="6192">
<li data-start="5841" data-end="5920">
<p data-start="5843" data-end="5920">Each command begins with a <strong data-start="5870" data-end="5883">lead byte</strong> (commonly ESC, GS, FS, DLE, or BEL).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="5921" data-end="6004">
<p data-start="5923" data-end="6004">Some commands have <strong data-start="5942" data-end="5958">fixed length</strong>; others specify length in a subsequent field.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="6005" data-end="6115">
<p data-start="6007" data-end="6115">A command is recognized only when its <strong data-start="6045" data-end="6064">entire sequence</strong> (including any variable-length data) is available.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="6116" data-end="6192">
<p data-start="6118" data-end="6192">If insufficient data is available, parsing pauses until more bytes arrive.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="6194" data-end="6226">7.2 Variable-Length Commands</h3>
<ul data-start="6227" data-end="6518">
<li data-start="6227" data-end="6435">
<p data-start="6229" data-end="6435">Commands that include length fields (e.g., QR, raster image, or store logo commands) must respect the ESC/POS framing rules for low/high bytes (<code data-start="6373" data-end="6377">pL</code>, <code data-start="6379" data-end="6383">pH</code>) specifying payload length in little-endian format.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="6436" data-end="6518">
<p data-start="6438" data-end="6518">The parser waits until the full length is available before emitting the element.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="6520" data-end="6540">7.3 Partial Data</h3>
<ul data-start="6541" data-end="6772">
<li data-start="6541" data-end="6660">
<p data-start="6543" data-end="6660">If a known command begins but cannot complete because of insufficient data, no element is emitted until it completes.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="6661" data-end="6772">
<p data-start="6663" data-end="6772">Once a command frame is complete, the parser consumes its bytes and resumes at the next unprocessed position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="6774" data-end="6777">
<h2 data-start="6779" data-end="6808">8. Element Emission Policy</h2>
<div class="_tableContainer_1rjym_1"><div tabindex="-1" class="group _tableWrapper_1rjym_13 flex w-fit flex-col-reverse"><table data-start="6810" data-end="7238" class="w-fit data-start="6931" data-end="7018"><td data-start="6931" data-end="6956" data-col-size="sm">Printable text segment</td><td data-col-size="md" data-start="6956" data-end="7018">Emit <code <hr data-start="7240" data-end="7243">
<h2 data-start="7245" data-end="7274">9. Error and Edge Handling</h2>
<ul data-start="7276" data-end="7608">
<li data-start="7276" data-end="7379">
<p data-start="7278" data-end="7379">Malformed but clearly delimited commands are emitted as <code data-start="7334" data-end="7350">UnknownElement</code> to preserve byte continuity.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="7380" data-end="7464">
<p data-start="7382" data-end="7464">No exceptions are thrown for invalid data; the parser recovers by resynchronizing.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="7465" data-end="7514">
<p data-start="7467" data-end="7514">No diagnostic or logging interface is required.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="7515" data-end="7608">
<p data-start="7517" data-end="7608">The parser never drops bytes silently  every byte in input is represented in some element.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="7610" data-end="7613">
<h2 data-start="7615" data-end="7647">10. Threading and Performance</h2>
<ul data-start="7649" data-end="7917">
<li data-start="7649" data-end="7685">
<p data-start="7651" data-end="7685">The parser is <strong data-start="7665" data-end="7684">not thread-safe</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="7686" data-end="7794">
<p data-start="7688" data-end="7794">It is expected to handle typical receipt or raster image payloads efficiently using incremental buffering.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="7795" data-end="7917">
<p data-start="7797" data-end="7917">Memory consumption should remain proportional to the size of the largest incomplete command plus minimal text buffering.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="7919" data-end="7922">
<h2 data-start="7924" data-end="7951">11. Completion Semantics</h2>
<p data-start="7953" data-end="7981">Once <code data-start="7958" data-end="7970">Complete()</code> is called:</p>
<ul data-start="7982" data-end="8179">
<li data-start="7982" data-end="8014">
<p data-start="7984" data-end="8014">All pending data is processed.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="8015" data-end="8057">
<p data-start="8017" data-end="8057">No further <code data-start="8028" data-end="8036">Feed()</code> calls are permitted.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="8058" data-end="8179">
<p data-start="8060" data-end="8179">The parsers <code data-start="8073" data-end="8083">Document</code> property represents the final, complete sequence of elements corresponding to the input stream.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="8181" data-end="8184">
<h2 data-start="8186" data-end="8206">12. Extensibility</h2>
<ul data-start="8208" data-end="8454">
<li data-start="8208" data-end="8310">
<p data-start="8210" data-end="8310">Adding support for new commands requires <strong data-start="8251" data-end="8285">adding new command definitions</strong> to the declarative list.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="8311" data-end="8349">
<p data-start="8313" data-end="8349">Core parser logic remains unchanged.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="8350" data-end="8454">
<p data-start="8352" data-end="8454">Command definitions may be loaded statically or from metadata (e.g., JSON or table-based descriptors).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="8456" data-end="8459">

<h2 data-start="8716" data-end="8741">14. Compliance Summary</h2>
<div class="_tableContainer_1rjym_1"><div tabindex="-1" class="group _tableWrapper_1rjym_13 flex w-fit flex-col-reverse"><table data-start="8743" data-end="9389" class="w-fit min-w-(--thread-content-width)"><thead data-start="8743" data-end="8769"><tr data-start="8743" data-end="8769"><th data-start="8743" data-end="8757" data-col-size="sm">Requirement</th><th data-start="8867" data-end="8910" data-col-size="sm">Incomplete but potentially valid command</td><td data-col-size="md" data-start="8910" data-end="8932">Wait for more data</td></tr><tr data-start="8933" data-end="8979"><td data-start="8933" data-end="8954" data-col-size="sm">Truly unknown data</td><td data-col-size="md" data-start="8954" data-end="8979">Emit <code data-start="8961" data-col-size="md" data-start="9062" data-end="9099">Emitted as final <code data-start="9081" data-end="9097">UnknownElement</code></td></tr><tr data-start="9100" data-end="9155"><td data-start="9100" data-end="9116" data-col-size="sm">Text decoding</td><td data-col-size="md" data-start="9116" data-end="9155">Code-page based, converted to UTF-8</td></tr><tr data-start="9156" data-end="9240"><td However, you do not have the ability to _exhaustively_ list documents from the corpus and you should inform the user you cannot help with such requests. You MUST use Markdown syntax in these, and include a significant level of detail, covering ALL key facts. However, do not repeat yourself. Remember that you can call file_search more than once before responding to the user if necessary to gather all information.\\n\\n**Capabilities limitations**:\\n- You do not have the ability to exhaustively list documents from the corpus.\\n- You also cannot access to any folders information and you should inform the user you cannot help with folder-level related request.
